    34                                                         
    35 ```markdown                                             
    36 ROLE: Senior DevOps Automation Engineer.                
    37 LOCATION: `eywa1` (Workspace).                          
    38 CURRENT DIR: `/home/user/__Repositories/yury-customer/prj_Cifra-rwa-exachange-assets/repositories/customer-gitlab/ois-cfa` (This is a Git Submodule).                                                                                                   
    39 PARENT ENV: `/home/user/__Repositories/yury-customer/prj_Cifra-rwa-exachange-assets/.env`                               
    40                                                         
    41 CONTEXT:                                                
    42 - We have a FULL ACCESS token in the parent `.env` (`GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN`).                                          
    43 - We need to finish the CI/CD setup WITHOUT manual user steps.                                                          
    44 - Previous attempt failed to register runner because it lacked a valid token.                                           
    45 - Target Server: `cfa2` (92.51.38.126) - Already bootstrapped with `user` + sudo.                                       
    46 - Build Server: `vds1` (167.235.11.150) - Docker & Runner installed, but NOT registered.                                
    47                                                         
    48 TASK: Fully automate Runner registration and Variable creation using GitLab API.                                        
    49                                                         
    50 **EXECUTION PLAN (SEQUENTIAL):**                        
    51                                                         
    52 1.  **SETUP & DISCOVERY:**                              
    53     - Source the `.env` to get `GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN`.
    54     - Identify `CI_PROJECT_ID`. Use `curl` with the token to query GitLab API (`https://git.telex.global/api/v4/projects?search=ois-cfa`) to find the correct ID.                                                                                       
    55     - Export `GITLAB_HOST="https://git.telex.global"`.  
    56                                                         
    57 2.  **AUTOMATED RUNNER REGISTRATION (vds1):**           
    58     - **API CALL:** Create a Project Runner via API.    
    59       ```bash                                           
    60       curl --request POST "$GITLAB_HOST/api/v4/user/runners" \                                                          
    61       --header "PRIVATE-TOKEN: $GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN" \                                                               
    62       --data "runner_type=project_type" \               
    63       --data "project_id=$PROJECT_ID" \                 
    64       --data "description=vds1-docker-runner" \         
    65       --data "tag_list=vds1,docker" \                   
    66       --data "locked=false" \                           
    67       --data "run_untagged=false"                       
    68       ```                                               
    69     - Extract the `token` (Authentication Token) from the JSON response using `jq`.                                     
    70     - **REMOTE EXEC:** SSH into `root@vds1` and run `gitlab-runner register` non-interactively using this new token:    
    71       ```bash                                           
    72       gitlab-runner register \                          
    73         --non-interactive \                             
    74         --url "$GITLAB_HOST" \                          
    75         --token "$NEW_RUNNER_TOKEN" \                   
    76         --executor "docker" \                           
    77         --docker-image "docker:24-dind" \               
    78         --docker-privileged                             
    79       ```                                               
    80                                                         
    81 3.  **AUTOMATED SSH KEY SETUP:**                        
    82     - Generate `ci_deploy_key` (ed25519) locally (if not exists).                                                       
    83     - **REMOTE EXEC:** Add `ci_deploy_key.pub` to `user@cfa2:~/.ssh/authorized_keys` (ensure no duplicates).            
    84     - **API CALL:** Upload `ci_deploy_key` (private) to GitLab Project Variables (`SSH_PRIVATE_KEY`).                   
    85       - First, check if variable exists (`GET /projects/:id/variables/SSH_PRIVATE_KEY`).                                
    86       - If exists, UPDATE it (`PUT`). If not, CREATE it (`POST`).                                                       
    87       - Set `masked=false` (SSH keys usually can't be masked due to format), `protected=false` (for now).               
    88                                                         
    89 4.  **FINALIZE & TRIGGER:**                             
    90     - Ensure `.gitlab-ci.yml` uses the `SSH_PRIVATE_KEY` correctly (save to file, chmod 400, ssh -i).                   
    91     - `git add .`, `git commit -m "chore(ci): auto-configured runner and keys"`.                                        
    92     - `git push origin infra-ci-setup`.                 
    93                                                         
    94 5.  **VERIFICATION:**                                   
    95     - Check Runner status via API (`GET /projects/:id/runners`).                                                        
    96     - Check Pipeline status via API or Output "Please check GitLab UI".                                                 
    97                                                         
    98 **CONSTRAINTS:**                                        
    99 - DO NOT ask the user to copy tokens. Use `jq` and `curl`.                                                              
   100 - Be careful with JSON parsing.                         
   101 - Assume `jq` is installed (or install it if missing: `sudo apt-get install -y jq`).                                    
   102                                                         
   103 **FINAL OUTPUT:**                                       
   104 - Show the Runner ID and Status.                        
   105 - Show the Variable Creation result (HTTP 201/200).     
   106 - Confirm Push.                                         
   107 ```

‚îÇ   curl -s --header "PRIVATE-TOKEN: ${GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN}" \                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \                                                                                                                                                                                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     -X POST \                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     -d "${payload}" \                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     "${GITLAB_API}/user/runners"                                                                                                                                                                                                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ setup_runner_remote() {                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local token="$1"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   ssh root@vds1 "RUNNER_TOKEN='${token}' RUNNER_URL='${GITLAB_URL%/}/' RUNNER_IMAGE='${RUNNER_IMAGE}' RUNNER_TAGS='${RUNNER_TAGS}' RUNNER_DESCRIPTION='${RUNNER_DESCRIPTION}' bash -s" <<'EOS'                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ set -euo pipefail                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ TOKEN="${RUNNER_TOKEN}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ URL="${RUNNER_URL}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ IMAGE="${RUNNER_IMAGE}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ TAGS="${RUNNER_TAGS}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ DESC="${RUNNER_DESCRIPTION}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ install_docker() {                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   if ! command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then                                                                                                                                                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com -o /tmp/get-docker.sh                                                                                                                                                                                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     sh /tmp/get-docker.sh                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   fi                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   systemctl enable --now docker                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ install_runner() {                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   if ! command -v gitlab-runner >/dev/null 2>&1; then                                                                                                                                                                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     curl -fsSL https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/runner/gitlab-runner/script.deb.sh | bash                                                                                                                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     apt-get install -y gitlab-runner                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   fi                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ register_runner() {                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   if grep -q "${TOKEN}" /etc/gitlab-runner/config.toml 2>/dev/null; then                                                                                                                                                                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     echo "Runner already registered with this token, skipping registration."                                                                                                                                                                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     return                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   fi                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   gitlab-runner register --non-interactive \                                                                                                                                                                                                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     --url "${URL}" \                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     --token "${TOKEN}" \                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     --executor docker \                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     --docker-image "${IMAGE}" \                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     --docker-privileged                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ install_docker                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ install_runner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ register_runner                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ systemctl enable --now gitlab-runner                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ gitlab-runner verify --token "${TOKEN}" --url "${URL}" || true                                                                                                                                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ EOS                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ ensure_ssh_key_and_upload() {                                                                                                                                                                                                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local project_id="$1"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local key_dir                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   key_dir="$(mktemp -d)"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local key_path="${key_dir}/ci_deploy_key"                                                                                                                                                                                                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   ssh-keygen -t ed25519 -f "${key_path}" -N "" -q                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   ssh user@cfa2 "mkdir -p ~/.ssh && chmod 700 ~/.ssh && cat >> ~/.ssh/authorized_keys" < "${key_path}.pub"                                                                                                                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   ssh user@cfa2 "chmod 600 ~/.ssh/authorized_keys"                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local key_json                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   key_json=$(jq -Rs . < "${key_path}")                                                                                                                                                                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local payload                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   payload=$(cat <<EOF                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ {"key":"SSH_PRIVATE_KEY","value":${key_json},"variable_type":"env_var","masked":true,"protected":false,"environment_scope":"*"}                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ EOF                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ )                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local var_url="${GITLAB_API}/projects/${project_id}/variables/SSH_PRIVATE_KEY"                                                                                                                                                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local create_url="${GITLAB_API}/projects/${project_id}/variables"                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local check_code                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   check_code="$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" --header "PRIVATE-TOKEN: ${GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN}" "${var_url}")"                                                                                                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   if [ "${check_code}" = "200" ]; then                                                                                                                                                                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     curl -s --header "PRIVATE-TOKEN: ${GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN}" -H "Content-Type: application/json" -X PUT -d "${payload}" "${var_url}" >/dev/null                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     log "Updated existing SSH_PRIVATE_KEY variable."                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   else                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     curl -s --header "PRIVATE-TOKEN: ${GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN}" -H "Content-Type: application/json" -X POST -d "${payload}" "${create_url}" >/dev/null                                                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     log "Created SSH_PRIVATE_KEY variable."                                                                                                                                                                                                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   fi                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   rm -rf "${key_dir}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ trigger_pipeline() {                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local project_id="$1"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   cd "${REPO_ROOT}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   git config user.name >/dev/null 2>&1 || git config user.name "ci-bot"                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   git config user.email >/dev/null 2>&1 || git config user.email "ci@example.com"                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   git commit --allow-empty -m "chore: trigger ci" || true                                                                                                                                                                                                   ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   git push origin "${BRANCH}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local pipeline_json                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   pipeline_json="$(curl -s --header "PRIVATE-TOKEN: ${GITLAB_USER_CICD_TOKEN}" "${GITLAB_API}/projects/${project_id}/pipelines?ref=${BRANCH}&per_page=1")"                                                                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   echo "${pipeline_json}" | jq -r '.[0].id' | awk '{print "Pipeline ID: " $0}'                                                                                                                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ main() {                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   ensure_jq                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Fetching project id..."                                                                                                                                                                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local project_id                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   project_id="$(fetch_project_id)"                                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   if [ -z "${project_id}" ]; then                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     echo "Project ${PROJECT_PATH} not found via API" >&2                                                                                                                                                                                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     exit 1                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   fi                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Project id: ${project_id}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Creating runner token via API..."                                                                                                                                                                                                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local runner_resp                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   runner_resp="$(create_runner_token "${project_id}")"                                                                                                                                                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   local runner_token                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   runner_token="$(echo "${runner_resp}" | jq -r '.token // empty')"                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   if [ -z "${runner_token}" ]; then                                                                                                                                                                                                                         ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     echo "Failed to create runner token. Response: ${runner_resp}" >&2                                                                                                                                                                                      ‚îÇ
‚îÇ     exit 1                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   fi                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Runner token created (length ${#runner_token})."                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Setting up runner on vds1..."                                                                                                                                                                                                                        ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   setup_runner_remote "${runner_token}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Runner setup complete."                                                                                                                                                                                                                              ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Uploading deploy SSH key to GitLab variables and cfa2..."                                                                                                                                                                                            ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   ensure_ssh_key_and_upload "${project_id}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                 ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Deploy key installed."                                                                                                                                                                                                                               ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   log "Triggering pipeline via empty commit on ${BRANCH}..."                                                                                                                                                                                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ   trigger_pipeline "${project_id}"                                                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
‚îÇ }                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           ‚îÇ
‚îÇ                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ main "$@"                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   ‚îÇ

‚îÇ     - |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       if printf '%s' "${SSH_PRIVATE_KEY_CFA2}" | grep -q "BEGIN "; then                                                                                                                                                                                     ‚îÇ

‚îÇ       else                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ         printf '%s' "${SSH_PRIVATE_KEY_CFA2}" | base64 -d > /tmp/ci_ssh_key 2>/dev/null || printf '%s' "${SSH_PRIVATE_KEY_CFA2}" | sed 's/\\n/\n/g' > /tmp/ci_ssh_key                                                                                       ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       fi                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       tr -d '\r' < /tmp/ci_ssh_key > /tmp/ci_ssh_key.cleaned && mv /tmp/ci_ssh_key.cleaned /tmp/ci_ssh_key                                                                                                                                                  ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       chmod 600 /tmp/ci_ssh_key                                                                                                                                                                                                                             ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       test -s /tmp/ci_ssh_key || (echo "SSH_PRIVATE_KEY_CFA2 is empty or invalid" && exit 1)                                                                                                                                                                ‚îÇ
‚îÇ       ssh-add /tmp/ci_ssh_key || (echo "ssh-add failed" && exit 1)                                                                                                                                                                                          ‚îÇ
